\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}Text with color / style.

Args:
    text (str, optional): Default unstyled text. Defaults to "".
    style (Union[str, Style], optional): Base style for text. Defaults to "".
    justify (str, optional): Justify method: "left", "center", "full", "right". Defaults to None.
    overflow (str, optional): Overflow method: "crop", "fold", "ellipsis". Defaults to None.
    no_wrap (bool, optional): Disable text wrapping, or None for default. Defaults to None.
    end (str, optional): Character to end text with. Defaults to "\\\\n".
    tab_size (int): Number of spaces per tab, or ``None`` to use ``console.tab_size``. Defaults to 8.
    spans (List[Span], optional). A list of predefined style spans. Defaults to None.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{text_8py_source_l00101}{101}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily  "{}Text"{} assemble (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{cls,  }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}Union\mbox{[}str, "{}Text"{}, Tuple\mbox{[}str, Style\+Type\mbox{]}\mbox{]}}]{parts,  }\item[{Union\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__vendor_1_1rich_1_1style_1_1Style}{Style}}\mbox{]} }]{style = {\ttfamily "{}"{}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}"{}Justify\+Method"{}\mbox{]} }]{justify = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}"{}Overflow\+Method"{}\mbox{]} }]{overflow = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}bool\mbox{]} }]{no\+\_\+wrap = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{str }]{end = {\ttfamily "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}},  }\item[{int }]{tab\+\_\+size = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}Dict\mbox{[}str, Any\mbox{]}\mbox{]} }]{meta = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Construct a text instance by combining a sequence of strings with optional styles.
The positional arguments should be either strings, or a tuple of string + style.

Args:
    style (Union[str, Style], optional): Base style for text. Defaults to "".
    justify (str, optional): Justify method: "left", "center", "full", "right". Defaults to None.
    overflow (str, optional): Overflow method: "crop", "fold", "ellipsis". Defaults to None.
    end (str, optional): Character to end text with. Defaults to "\\\\n".
    tab_size (int): Number of spaces per tab, or ``None`` to use ``console.tab_size``. Defaults to 8.
    meta (Dict[str, Any], optional). Meta data to apply to text, or None for no meta data. Default to None

Returns:
    Text: A new text instance.
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily  "{}Text"{} from\+\_\+ansi (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{cls,  }\item[{str}]{text,  }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}Union\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__vendor_1_1rich_1_1style_1_1Style}{Style}}\mbox{]} }]{style = {\ttfamily "{}"{}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}"{}Justify\+Method"{}\mbox{]} }]{justify = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}"{}Overflow\+Method"{}\mbox{]} }]{overflow = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}bool\mbox{]} }]{no\+\_\+wrap = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{str }]{end = {\ttfamily "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}int\mbox{]} }]{tab\+\_\+size = {\ttfamily 8} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Create a Text object from a string containing ANSI escape codes.

Args:
    text (str): A string containing escape codes.
    style (Union[str, Style], optional): Base style for text. Defaults to "".
    justify (str, optional): Justify method: "left", "center", "full", "right". Defaults to None.
    overflow (str, optional): Overflow method: "crop", "fold", "ellipsis". Defaults to None.
    no_wrap (bool, optional): Disable text wrapping, or None for default. Defaults to None.
    end (str, optional): Character to end text with. Defaults to "\\\\n".
    tab_size (int): Number of spaces per tab, or ``None`` to use ``console.tab_size``. Defaults to 8.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\index{Text@{Text}!on@{on}}
\index{on@{on}!Text@{Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{on()}{on()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily  "{}Text"{} on (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self,  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}Dict\mbox{[}str, Any\mbox{]}\mbox{]} }]{meta = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}Any}]{handlers }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Apply event handlers (used by Textual project).

Example:
    >>> from rich.text import Text
    >>> text = Text("hello world")
    >>> text.on(click="view.toggle('world')")

Args:
    meta (Dict[str, Any]): Mapping of meta information.
    **handlers: Keyword args are prefixed with "@" to defined handlers.

Returns:
    Text: Self is returned to method may be chained.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Split rich text in to lines, preserving styles.

Args:
    separator (str, optional): String to split on. Defaults to "\\\\n".
    include_separator (bool, optional): Include the separator in the lines. Defaults to False.
    allow_blank (bool, optional): Return a blank line if the text ends with a separator. Defaults to False.

Returns:
    List[RichText]: A list of rich text, one per line of the original.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Construct a Text instance with a pre-applied styled. A style applied in this way won't be used
to pad the text when it is justified.

Args:
    text (str): A string containing console markup.
    style (Union[str, Style]): Style to apply to the text. Defaults to "".
    justify (str, optional): Justify method: "left", "center", "full", "right". Defaults to None.
    overflow (str, optional): Overflow method: "crop", "fold", "ellipsis". Defaults to None.

Returns:
    Text: A text instance with a style applied to the entire string.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wrap()}{wrap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily  \mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__vendor_1_1rich_1_1containers_1_1Lines}{Lines}} wrap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self,  }\item[{"{}Console"{}}]{console,  }\item[{int}]{width,  }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}Optional\mbox{[}"{}Justify\+Method"{}\mbox{]} }]{justify = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}"{}Overflow\+Method"{}\mbox{]} }]{overflow = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}},  }\item[{int }]{tab\+\_\+size = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}bool\mbox{]} }]{no\+\_\+wrap = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Word wrap the text.

Args:
    console (Console): Console instance.
    width (int): Number of characters per line.
    emoji (bool, optional): Also render emoji code. Defaults to True.
    justify (str, optional): Justify method: "default", "left", "center", "full", "right". Defaults to "default".
    overflow (str, optional): Overflow method: "crop", "fold", or "ellipsis". Defaults to None.
    tab_size (int, optional): Default tab size. Defaults to 8.
    no_wrap (bool, optional): Disable wrapping, Defaults to False.

Returns:
    Lines: Number of lines.
\end{DoxyVerb}
